            configs={"config.yaml": module_schema(os_name="linux", actions=[])},
        )
        write_module(
            tmp_path,
            "common",
            configs={"config.yaml": module_schema(actions=[])},
        )

        assert result.returncode == 0, result.stderr
        payload = parse_stdout_json(result)

entrypoint_argv = ['uv', 'run', '--project', '/workspace', '/workspace/rig.py']
tmp_path = PosixPath('/tmp/pytest-of-agent/pytest-0/test_validate_rejects_invalid_14')
config_payload = {'actions': 'copy', 'schema': 'module', 'version': '1'}
expected_error_parts = ('actions', 'list')

    @pytest.mark.error
    @pytest.mark.parametrize(
        ("config_payload", "expected_error_parts"),
        [
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1"},
                ("schema", "required"),
                id="schema-required",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "unknown_schema"},
                ("schema", "unknown_schema"),
                id="schema-unrecognized",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": 1},
                ("schema", "string"),
                id="schema-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "module", "os": "linux"},
                ("os", "object"),
                id="os-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "module", "os": {}},
                ("os.name", "required"),
                id="os-name-required",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "module", "os": {"name": "windows"}},
                ("os.name", "macos", "linux"),
                id="os-name-invalid",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {"name": "linux", "package_manager": "pacman"},
                },
                ("os.package_manager", "brew", "apt", "yum"),
                id="package-manager-invalid",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "packages": "curl",
                    },
                },
                ("os.packages", "list"),
                id="packages-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "packages": [1],
                    },
                },
                ("os.packages[0]", "string"),
                id="packages-item-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "packages": [""],
                    },
                },
                ("os.packages[0]", "non-empty"),
                id="packages-item-empty",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "applications": "firefox",
                    },
                },
                ("os.applications", "list"),
                id="applications-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "applications": [1],
                    },
                },
                ("os.applications[0]", "string"),
                id="applications-item-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "os": {
                        "name": "linux",
                        "package_manager": "apt",
                        "applications": [""],
                    },
                },
                ("os.applications[0]", "non-empty"),
                id="applications-item-empty",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {

                ("os.package_manager", "required", "applications"),
                id="package-manager-required-with-apps",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "module", "actions": "copy"},

            ),
            pytest.param(

                id="action-item-type",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",

                id="action-type-required",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "actions": [{"type": 1, "source": "file.sh"}],
                },
                ("actions[0].type", "string"),
                id="action-type-string",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",
                    "schema": "module",
                    "actions": [{"type": "move", "source": "file.sh"}],
                },
                ("actions[0].type", "move"),
                id="action-type-unknown",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {"version": "1", "schema": "module", "actions": [{"type": "run"}]},
                ("actions[0].source", "required"),
                id="action-source-required",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",

                id="action-source-string",
            ),
            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",

            ),
            pytest.param(

                    "version": "1",

            pytest.param(
                {
                    "version": "1",

            ),

            ),

                id="destination-string",
            ),

                            "type": "copy",

                            "destination": "~/a",
                            "hidden": "yes",
                        }
                    ],
                },
                ("actions[0].hidden", "boolean"),
                id="hidden-type",

    def raw_decode(self, s, idx=0):
        """Decode a JSON document from ``s`` (a ``str`` beginning with
        a JSON document) and return a 2-tuple of the Python
        representation and the index in ``s`` where the document ended.

                            "destination": "~/.gitconfig",
                        },

            },

        )
